════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  Semantic FDP Data Placement Strategy
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

  PID 0: ACCOUNT_STATE (/home/femu/f2fs_fdp_mount/account_state)
  ├── High churn, mutable data
  ├── authorities_db/
  │   ├── objects (object state - frequently updated)
  │   ├── owned_object_transaction_locks (very high churn)
  │   └── object_per_epoch_marker_table (pruned per epoch)
  └── epoch_db/ (rotates each epoch)

  PID 1: LEDGER (/home/femu/f2fs_fdp_mount/ledger)
  ├── Append-only, immutable data
  ├── authorities_db/
  │   ├── transactions (write-once, never modified)
  │   ├── effects (write-once, never modified)
  │   └── events (append-only)
  ├── consensus_db/
  │   ├── blocks (append-only DAG)
  │   ├── commits (append-only)
  │   └── votes (append-only)
  └── full_node_db/
      ├── checkpoints (append-only)
      └── indexes (read-heavy)

════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  Why This Works Better Than LSM-Level Separation
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

  LSM-Level (Old Approach):
    - Separates by file SIZE (L0/L1 vs L4+)
    - RocksDB db_paths uses capacity overflow, NOT level assignment
    - Hot account data and hot ledger data STILL mix together
    - GC improvement is indirect and unreliable

  Semantic-Level (New Approach):
    - Separates by DATA CHARACTERISTICS
    - Account state: high update/delete rate → high GC
    - Ledger data: append-only → minimal GC
    - True lifetime isolation → no interference

════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  Usage Instructions
════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

1. Set environment variables before starting SUI:

   export SUI_FDP_SEMANTIC=1
   export SUI_FDP_BASE_PATH=/home/femu/f2fs_fdp_mount

2. Mount F2FS with only 2 FDP streams (simpler!):

   sudo /home/femu/fdp-scripts/f2fs-tools-fdp/fdp_send_sungjin /dev/nvme0n1
   sudo /home/femu/fdp-scripts/f2fs-tools-fdp/mkfs/mkfs.f2fs -f -O lost_found /dev/nvme0n1
   sudo mount -t f2fs -o fdp_log_n=2 /dev/nvme0n1 /home/femu/f2fs_fdp_mount

3. Start SUI node normally - it will use semantic FDP automatically
